.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eXP系统下运行说明\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca Go bindings for Sciter","## 更新到Sciter v6.0.4.5","## 兼容XP","## sciter sdk下载:","https://gitlab.com/sciter-engine/sciter-js-sdk/-/releases","","## 本仓库的代码兼容XP系统","","## 版本说明","已经更新到了v6的版本","根目录下的sciter.dll是v6.0.4.5的,截止2026-07-05最新版本","","## 编译提前配置","### 64位","先下载gcc 64位版本,设置环境变量PATH","set PATH=D:\\5CPP\\5.C\\mingw64\\bin;%PATH%;","","```shell","REM 64位","@echo off","chcp 65001","set PATH=E:\\go\\resources\\go-sciter\\xp\\w64devkit-x86-2.0.0\\bin;%PATH%;","set GOOS=windows","set GOARCH=amd64","set CGO_ENABLED=1","```","","### 32位XP","- 需要先下载 go 1.11.13-386 32位版本,这是测试过支持XP的最后版本,可以使用go module","- 下载gcc 32位,推荐w64devkit-x86-2.0.0,支持最新的XP系统的GCC","","```shell","REM 32位XP","@echo off","chcp 65001","set PATH=E:\\go\\resources\\go-sciter\\xp\\w64devkit-x86-2.0.0\\bin;%PATH%;","set GOOS=windows","set GOARCH=386","set CGO_ENABLED=1","```","","## 开始编译示例代码","\u003e go-sciter-demo 里面是最全的,其他的示例还没修改成兼容,只有以下2个示例是可以运行的,go-sciter-demo其中包含了其他全部","","- go build -x -o ./examples/callback/callback.exe ./examples/callback","- go build -x -o ./examples/go-sciter-demo/go-sciter-demo.exe ./examples/go-sciter-demo","","\u003e -x 表示显示中间的过程","\u003e ","\u003e -a 可以强制重新编译","\u003e ","\u003e -o 指定输出文件名","\u003e ","\u003e go-sciter-demo 的代码来自于:","https://github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter","\u003e 特别感谢","","## 运行特别注意","- 运行时,需要复制项目dll目录下对应的操作系统的sciter库到程序运行目录","- 32位的非XP系统,复制`dll\\windows\\x32\\sciter.dll`到程序运行目录","- 64位的系统,复制`dll\\windows\\x64\\sciter.dll`到程序运行目录","- xp系统,复制`dll\\windows.xp\\x32\\sciter.dll`到程序运行目录","- 其他系统类似","\u003e 此dll目录是官方sdk中bin目录复制的","","## dll目录下的 inspector.exe 是运行调试工具,类似于浏览器的开发者工具","","","## 程序运行时去掉黑框(cmd窗口)(建议在发布时使用)","没有黑色窗口,log.println或fmt.println就都看不到了","","在编译时加上参数 -ldflags=\"-H windowsgui\"，比如","","`go build -ldflags=\"-H windowsgui\"`","","## 自定义程序图标及版本信息","在没有使用winres时,go build的exe程序是没有图标及版本信息的.现在介绍使用方法(此方法只在windows下有效)","详细见: https://gitee.com/ying32/govcl/wikis/pages?sort_id=410058\u0026doc_id=102420","### 补充说明:","- app.rc包含了app.manifest(清单文件,可控制是否要管理员权限),applogo.ico(图标),版本信息(自定义)","- 编译命令(将rc转.syso)","* x86","  windres.exe -i app.rc -o defaultRes_windows_386.syso -F pe-i386","* x64","  windres.exe -i app.rc -o defaultRes_windows_amd64.syso -F pe-x86-64","- 编译后,只需要将.syso(名称无所谓,只能有一个,会默认找.syso)存放到项目根目录,就可以了,go build编译时,需要指定整个目录 go build .","","## XP系统下运行说明","### 解决XP中文乱码问题","","在所有公共的css或者当前页面头上添加:","","```css","html {","}","","* {","    font-family: \"SimSun\", \"宋体\",","    \"SimHei\", \"黑体\",","    \"Microsoft YaHei\", \"微软雅黑\",","    \"PingFang SC\",","    Tahoma, Arial, sans-serif !important;","}","```","","不知道为什么,必须在**html空标签后面设置**才会生效:","","### sqlite","运行sqlite时,会出现 无法定位程序输入点 ReleaseSWLockExcluseive 于动态链接库 KERNEL32.DLL 上","即使使用官方的scapp.exe也是同样的错误,并不是go的原因","因为,在官方的 bin\\windows.xp\\x32 目录下,就没有 sciter-sqlite.dll,所以,XP不支持,要想支持只能买源码,手动编译","- 但,GO可以使用GO的sqlite库,不使用sciter的","","## 以下是原readme","","[![AppVeyor status](https://ci.appveyor.com/api/projects/status/rphv883klffw9em9/branch/master?svg=true)](https://ci.appveyor.com/project/pravic/go-sciter)","[![Travis Status](https://travis-ci.com/sciter-sdk/go-sciter.svg?branch=master)](https://travis-ci.com/sciter-sdk/go-sciter)","[![License](https://img.shields.io/github/license/sciter-sdk/go-sciter.svg)](https://github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter)","[![Join the forums at https://sciter.com/forums](https://img.shields.io/badge/forum-sciter.com-orange.svg)](https://sciter.com/forums)","","Check [this page](http://sciter.com/developers/sciter-sdk-bindings/) for other language bindings (Delphi / D / Go / .NET / Python / Rust).","","----","","","# Attention","","The ownership of project is transferred to this new organization.","Thus the `import path` for golang should now be `github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter`, but the package name is still `sciter`.","","# Introduction","","This package provides a Golang bindings of [Sciter][] using cgo.","Using go sciter you must have the platform specified `sciter dynamic library`","downloaded from [sciter-sdk][], the library itself is rather small"," (under 5MB, less than 2MB when upxed) .","","Most [Sciter][] API are supported, including:",""," * Html string/file loading"," * DOM manipulation/callback/event handling"," * DOM state/attribute handling"," * Custom resource loading"," * Sciter Behavior"," * Sciter Options"," * Sciter Value support"," * NativeFunctor (used in sciter scripting)","","And the API are organized in more or less a gopher friendly way.","","Things that are not supported:",""," * Sciter Node API"," * TIScript Engine API","","# Getting Started","","###  At the moment only **Go 1.10** or higher is supported (issue #136).",""," 1. Download the [sciter-sdk][]"," 2. Extract the sciter runtime library from [sciter-sdk][] to system PATH","","    The runtime libraries lives in `bin` `bin.lnx` `bin.osx` with suffix like `dll` `so` or `dylib`","","    * Windows: simply copying `bin\\64\\sciter.dll` to `c:\\windows\\system32` is just enough","    * Linux:","      - `cd sciter-sdk/bin.lnx/x64`","      - `export LIBRARY_PATH=$PWD`","      - `echo $PWD \u003e\u003e libsciter.conf`","      - `sudo cp libsciter.conf /etc/ld.so.conf.d/`","      - `sudo ldconfig`","      - `ldconfig -p | grep sciter` should print libsciter-gtk.so location","    * OSX:","      - `cd sciter-sdk/bin.osx/`","      - `export DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH=$PWD`",""," 3. Set up GCC envrionmnet for CGO","","    [mingw64-gcc][] (5.2.0 and 7.2.0 are tested) is recommended for Windows users.","","    Under Linux gcc(4.8 or above) and gtk+-3.0 are needed.",""," 4. `go get -x github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter`",""," 5. Run the example and enjoy :)","","# Sciter Desktop UI Examples","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-wt5.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-norton360.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-norton-nis.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-cardio.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-surveillance.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-technology.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-sciter-ide.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-sciter-osx.png)","","![](http://sciter.com/screenshots/slide-sciter-gtk.png)","","","# Sciter Version Support","Currently supports [Sciter][] version `4.0.0.0` and higher.","","[Sciter]: http://sciter.com/","[sciter-sdk]: http://sciter.com/download/","","# About Sciter","","[Sciter][] is an `Embeddable HTML/CSS/script engine for modern UI development, Web designers, and developers, can reuse their experience and expertise in creating modern looking desktop applications.`","","In my opinion, [Sciter][] , though not open sourced, is an great","desktop UI development envrionment using the full stack of web technologies,","which is rather small (under 5MB) especially compared to [CEF][],[Node Webkit][nw] and [Atom Electron][electron]. :)","","Finally, according to [Andrew Fedoniouk][author] the author and the Sciter","`END USER LICENSE AGREEMENT` , the binary form of the [Sciter][]","dynamic libraries are totally free to use for commercial or","non-commercial applications.","","# The Tailored Sciter C Headers","This binding ueses a tailored version of the sciter C Headers, which lives in directory: `include`. The included c headers are a modified version of the","[sciter-sdk][] standard headers.","","It seems [Sciter][] is developed using C++, and the included headers in the","[Sciter SDK][sciter-sdk] are a mixture of C and C++, which is not","quite suitable for an easy golang binding.","","I'm not much fond of C++ since I started to use Golang, so I made this","modification and hope [Andrew <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">64位</h3><a id="user-content-64位" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 64位" href="#64位"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">先下载gcc 64位版本,设置环境变量PATH
set PATH=D:\5CPP\5.C\mingw64\bin;%PATH%;</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="REM 64位
@echo off
chcp 65001
set PATH=E:\go\resources\go-sciter\xp\w64devkit-x86-2.0.0\bin;%PATH%;
set GOOS=windows
set GOARCH=amd64
set CGO_ENABLED=1"><pre>REM 64位
@echo off
chcp 65001
<span class="pl-c1">set</span> PATH=E:<span class="pl-cce">\g</span>o<span class="pl-cce">\r</span>esources<span class="pl-cce">\g</span>o-sciter<span class="pl-cce">\x</span>p<span class="pl-cce">\w</span>64devkit-x86-2.0.0<span class="pl-cce">\b</span>in<span class="pl-k">;</span>%PATH%<span class="pl-k">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">32位XP</h3><a id="user-content-32位xp" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 32位XP" href="#32位xp"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>需要先下载 go 1.11.13-386 32位版本,这是测试过支持XP的最后版本,可以使用go module</li>
<li>下载gcc 32位,推荐w64devkit-x86-2.0.0,支持最新的XP系统的GCC</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="REM 32位XP
@echo off
chcp 65001
set PATH=E:\go\resources\go-sciter\xp\w64devkit-x86-2.0.0\bin;%PATH%;

set GOARCH=386
set CGO_ENABLED=1"><pre>REM 32位XP
@echo off
chcp 65001
<span class="pl-c1">set</span> PATH=E:<span class="pl-cce">\g</span>o<span class="pl-cce">\r</span>esources<span class="pl-cce">\g</span>o-sciter<span class="pl-cce">\x</span>p<span class="pl-cce">\w</span>64devkit-x86-2.0.0<span class="pl-cce">\b</span>in<span class="pl-k">;</span>%PATH%<span class="pl-k">;</span>

<span class="pl-c1">set</span> GOARCH=386
<span class="pl-c1">set</span> CGO_ENABLED=1</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">开始编译示例代码</h2><a id="user-content-开始编译示例代码" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 开始编译示例代码" href="#开始编译示例代码"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">go-sciter-demo 里面是最全的,其他的示例还没修改成兼容,只有以下2个示例是可以运行的,go-sciter-demo其中包含了其他全部</p>
</blockquote>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>go build -x -o ./examples/callback/callback.exe ./examples/callback</li>
<li>go build -x -o ./examples/go-sciter-demo/go-sciter-demo.exe ./examples/go-sciter-demo</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">-x 表示显示中间的过程</p>
<p dir="auto">-a 可以强制重新编译</p>
<p dir="auto">-o 指定输出文件名</p>
<p dir="auto">go-sciter-demo 的代码来自于:
<a href="https://github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter">https://github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter</a>
特别感谢</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">运行特别注意</h2><a id="user-content-运行特别注意" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 运行特别注意" href="#运行特别注意"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>运行时,需要复制项目dll目录下对应的操作系统的sciter库到程序运行目录</li>
<li>32位的非XP系统,复制<code>dll\windows\x32\sciter.dll</code>到程序运行目录</li>
<li>64位的系统,复制<code>dll\windows\x64\sciter.dll</code>到程序运行目录</li>
<li>xp系统,复制<code>dll\windows.xp\x32\sciter.dll</code>到程序运行目录</li>
<li>其他系统类似</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">此dll目录是官方sdk中bin目录复制的</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">dll目录下的 inspector.exe 是运行调试工具,类似于浏览器的开发者工具</h2><a id="user-content-dll目录下的-inspectorexe-是运行调试工具类似于浏览器的开发者工具" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: dll目录下的 inspector.exe 是运行调试工具,类似于浏览器的开发者工具" href="#dll目录下的-inspectorexe-是运行调试工具类似于浏览器的开发者工具"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">程序运行时去掉黑框(cmd窗口)(建议在发布时使用)</h2><a id="user-content-程序运行时去掉黑框cmd窗口建议在发布时使用" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 程序运行时去掉黑框(cmd窗口)(建议在发布时使用)" href="#程序运行时去掉黑框cmd窗口建议在发布时使用"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">没有黑色窗口,log.println或fmt.println就都看不到了</p>
<p dir="auto">在编译时加上参数 -ldflags="-H windowsgui"，比如</p>
<p dir="auto"><code>go build -ldflags="-H windowsgui"</code></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">自定义程序图标及版本信息</h2><a id="user-content-自定义程序图标及版本信息" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 自定义程序图标及版本信息" href="#自定义程序图标及版本信息"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">在没有使用winres时,go build的exe程序是没有图标及版本信息的.现在介绍使用方法(此方法只在windows下有效)
详细见: <a href="https://gitee.com/ying32/govcl/wikis/pages?sort_id=410058&amp;doc_id=102420" rel="nofollow">https://gitee.com/ying32/govcl/wikis/pages?sort_id=410058&amp;doc_id=102420</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">补充说明:</h3><a id="user-content-补充说明" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 补充说明:" href="#补充说明"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>app.rc包含了app.manifest(清单文件,可控制是否要管理员权限),applogo.ico(图标),版本信息(自定义)</li>
<li>编译命令(将rc转.syso)</li>
</ul>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>x86
windres.exe -i app.rc -o defaultRes_windows_386.syso -F pe-i386</li>
<li>x64
windres.exe -i app.rc -o defaultRes_windows_amd64.syso -F pe-x86-64</li>
</ul>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>编译后,只需要将.syso(名称无所谓,只能有一个,会默认找.syso)存放到项目根目录,就可以了,go build编译时,需要指定整个目录 go build .</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">XP系统下运行说明</h2><a id="user-content-xp系统下运行说明" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: XP系统下运行说明" href="#xp系统下运行说明"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">解决XP中文乱码问题</h3><a id="user-content-解决xp中文乱码问题" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 解决XP中文乱码问题" href="#解决xp中文乱码问题"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">在所有公共的css或者当前页面头上添加:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="html {
}

* {
    font-family: &quot;SimSun&quot;, &quot;宋体&quot;,
    &quot;SimHei&quot;, &quot;黑体&quot;,
    &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,
    &quot;PingFang SC&quot;,
    Tahoma, Arial, sans-serif !important;
}"><pre><span class="pl-ent">html</span> {
}

<span class="pl-ent"><span class="pl-c1">*</span></span> {
    <span class="pl-c1">font-family</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-s">"SimSun"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"宋体"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"SimHei"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"黑体"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"Microsoft YaHei"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s">"微软雅黑"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"PingFang SC"</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
    Tahoma<span class="pl-kos">,</span> Arial<span class="pl-kos">,</span> sans-serif <span class="pl-k">!important</span>;
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">不知道为什么,必须在<strong>html空标签后面设置</strong>才会生效:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">sqlite</h3><a id="user-content-sqlite" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: sqlite" href="#sqlite"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">运行sqlite时,会出现 无法定位程序输入点 ReleaseSWLockExcluseive 于动态链接库 KERNEL32.DLL 上
即使使用官方的scapp.exe也是同样的错误,并不是go的原因
因为,在官方的 bin\windows.xp\x32 目录下,就没有 sciter-sqlite.dll,所以,XP不支持,要想支持只能买源码,手动编译</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>但,GO可以使用GO的sqlite库,不使用sciter的</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">以下是原readme</h2><a id="user-content-以下是原readme" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 以下是原readme" href="#以下是原readme"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://ci.appveyor.com/project/pravic/go-sciter" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/61d973ab7e6ab4c618c320cdb3f265b96530b979a9ee487335436dee3cd26812/68747470733a2f2f63692e6170707665796f722e636f6d2f6170692f70726f6a656374732f7374617475732f727068763838336b6c66667739656d392f6272616e63682f6d61737465723f7376673d74727565" alt="AppVeyor status" data-canonical-src="https://ci.appveyor.com/api/projects/status/rphv883klffw9em9/branch/master?svg=true" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<a href="https://github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3568e6ac75cf995c2e52c54de42c1d3cd7c7daf46b44b38d62a48467f011a000/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6769746875622f6c6963656e73652f7363697465722d73646b2f676f2d7363697465722e737667" alt="License" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/github/license/sciter-sdk/go-sciter.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<p dir="auto">Check <a href="http://sciter.com/developers/sciter-sdk-bindings/" rel="nofollow">this page</a> for other language bindings (Delphi / D / Go / .NET / Python / Rust).</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Attention</h1><a id="user-content-attention" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Attention" href="#attention"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The ownership of project is transferred to this new organization.
Thus the <code>import path</code> for golang should now be <code>github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter</code>, but the package name is still <code>sciter</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Introduction</h1><a id="user-content-introduction" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Introduction" href="#introduction"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This package provides a Golang bindings of <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> using cgo.
Using go sciter you must have the platform specified <code>sciter dynamic library</code>
downloaded from <a href="http://sciter.com/download/" rel="nofollow">sciter-sdk</a>, the library itself is rather small
(under 5MB, less than 2MB when upxed) .</p>
<p dir="auto">Most <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> API are supported, including:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Html string/file loading</li>
<li>DOM manipulation/callback/event handling</li>
<li>DOM state/attribute handling</li>
<li>Custom resource loading</li>
<li>Sciter Behavior</li>
<li>Sciter Options</li>
<li>Sciter Value support</li>
<li>NativeFunctor (used in sciter scripting)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">And the API are organized in more or less a gopher friendly way.</p>
<p dir="auto">Things that are not supported:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Sciter Node API</li>
<li>TIScript Engine API</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Getting Started</h1><a id="user-content-getting-started" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Getting Started" href="#getting-started"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">At the moment only <strong>Go 1.10</strong> or higher is supported (issue #136).</h3><a id="user-content-at-the-moment-only-go-110-or-higher-is-supported-issue-136" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: At the moment only Go 1.10 or higher is supported (issue #136)." href="#at-the-moment-only-go-110-or-higher-is-supported-issue-136"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Download the <a href="http://sciter.com/download/" rel="nofollow">sciter-sdk</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Extract the sciter runtime library from <a href="http://sciter.com/download/" rel="nofollow">sciter-sdk</a> to system PATH</p>
<p dir="auto">The runtime libraries lives in <code>bin</code> <code>bin.lnx</code> <code>bin.osx</code> with suffix like <code>dll</code> <code>so</code> or <code>dylib</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Windows: simply copying <code>bin\64\sciter.dll</code> to <code>c:\windows\system32</code> is just enough</li>
<li>Linux:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>cd sciter-sdk/bin.lnx/x64</code></li>
<li><code>export LIBRARY_PATH=$PWD</code></li>
<li><code>echo $PWD &gt;&gt; libsciter.conf</code></li>
<li><code>sudo cp libsciter.conf /etc/ld.so.conf.d/</code></li>
<li><code>sudo ldconfig</code></li>
<li><code>ldconfig -p | grep sciter</code> should print libsciter-gtk.so location</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>OSX:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>cd sciter-sdk/bin.osx/</code></li>
<li><code>export DYLD_LIBRARY_PATH=$PWD</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Set up GCC envrionmnet for CGO</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="http://sourceforge.net/projects/mingw-w64/" rel="nofollow">mingw64-gcc</a> (5.2.0 and 7.2.0 are tested) is recommended for Windows users.</p>
<p dir="auto">Under Linux gcc(4.8 or above) and gtk+-3.0 are needed.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>go get -x github.com/Mr-ShiHuaYu/go-sciter</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Run the example and enjoy :)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sciter Desktop UI Examples</h1><a id="user-content-sciter-desktop-ui-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sciter Desktop UI Examples" href="#sciter-desktop-ui-examples"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sciter Version Support</h1><a id="user-content-sciter-version-support" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sciter Version Support" href="#sciter-version-support"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Currently supports <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> version <code>4.0.0.0</code> and higher.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">About Sciter</h1><a id="user-content-about-sciter" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: About Sciter" href="#about-sciter"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> is an <code>Embeddable HTML/CSS/script engine for modern UI development, Web designers, and developers, can reuse their experience and expertise in creating modern looking desktop applications.</code></p>
<p dir="auto">In my opinion, <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> , though not open sourced, is an great
desktop UI development envrionment using the full stack of web technologies,
which is rather small (under 5MB) especially compared to <a href="https://bitbucket.org/chromiumembedded/cef" rel="nofollow">CEF</a>,<a href="https://github.com/nwjs/nw.js">Node Webkit</a> and <a href="https://github.com/atom/electron">Atom Electron</a>. :)</p>
<p dir="auto">Finally, according to <a href="http://sciter.com/about/" rel="nofollow">Andrew Fedoniouk</a> the author and the Sciter
<code>END USER LICENSE AGREEMENT</code> , the binary form of the <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a>
dynamic libraries are totally free to use for commercial or
non-commercial applications.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The Tailored Sciter C Headers</h1><a id="user-content-the-tailored-sciter-c-headers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The Tailored Sciter C Headers" href="#the-tailored-sciter-c-headers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This binding ueses a tailored version of the sciter C Headers, which lives in directory: <code>include</code>. The included c headers are a modified version of the
<a href="http://sciter.com/download/" rel="nofollow">sciter-sdk</a> standard headers.</p>
<p dir="auto">It seems <a href="http://sciter.com/" rel="nofollow">Sciter</a> is developed using C++, and the included headers in the
<a href="http://sciter.com/download/" rel="nofollow">Sciter SDK</a> are a mixture of C and C++, which is not
quite suitable for an easy golang binding.</p>
<p dir="auto">I'm not much fond of C++ since I started to use Golang, so I made this
modification and hope <a href="http://sciter.com/about/" rel="nofollow">Andrew Fedoniouk</a> the author would provide
pure C header files for Sciter. :)</p>
</article></div><div class="d-none"></div></section></div></div></div> </div> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ScrollMarksContainer-module__scrollMarksContainer__Eu7uU" id="find-result-marks-container"></div><div class="d-none"></div><div class="d-none"></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> </div>
</react-app>




  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>

  </div>
